var ykQHeader = {
	ltrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /^(\s*|ã*)/, "") },
	rtrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /(\s*|ã*)$/, "") },
	trim:function(s){ return this.ltrim(this.rtrim(s));},
	doSearch: function () {
		this.form = document.getElementById('qheader_search');
		if(!this.form){ return; }
		this.input = this.form.getElementsByTagName('input')[0];
		var q = this.trim(this.input.value), url = '',
				stat = 'spm=a2hww.20023042.#qheader_search~10';
		if (window.logPvid) {
			stat += '&_rp=' + window.logPvid;
		}

		if (q == '') {
			url = '//www.soku.com?inner' + ('&' + stat);
		} else {
			if (this.form.action.indexOf('/q_') === -1) {
				q = encodeURIComponent(q);
				url = this.form.action + '/q_' + q + ('?' + stat);
			} else {
				url = this.form.action + ('&' + stat);
			}
		}
		window.open(url);
		this.form.action = '//www.soku.com/search_video';
		return false;
	}
}

	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>

	ltrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /^(\s*|ã*)/, "") },
	rtrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /(\s*|ã*)$/, "") },
	trim:function(s){ return this.ltrim(this.rtrim(s));},
	doSearch: function () {
		this.form = document.getElementById('qheader_search');
		if(!this.form){ return; }
		this.input = this.form.getElementsByTagName('input')[0];
		var q = this.trim(this.input.value), url = '',
				stat = 'spm=a2hww.20023042.#qheader_search~10';
		if (window.logPvid) {
			stat += '&_rp=' + window.logPvid;
		}

		if (q == '') {
			url = '//www.soku.com?inner' + ('&' + stat);
		} else {
			if (this.form.action.indexOf('/q_') === -1) {
				q = encodeURIComponent(q);
				url = this.form.action + '/q_' + q + ('?' + stat);
			} else {
				url = this.form.action + ('&' + stat);
			}
		}
		window.open(url);
		this.form.action = '//www.soku.com/search_video';
		return false;
	}
}

	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>

var ykQHeader = {
	ltrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /^(\s*|ã*)/, "") },
	rtrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /(\s*|ã*)$/, "") },
	trim:function(s){ return this.ltrim(this.rtrim(s));},
	doSearch: function () {
		this.form = document.getElementById('qheader_search');
		if(!this.form){ return; }
		this.input = this.form.getElementsByTagName('input')[0];
		var q = this.trim(this.input.value), url = '',
				stat = 'spm=a2hww.20023042.#qheader_search~10';
		if (window.logPvid) {
			stat += '&_rp=' + window.logPvid;
		}

		if (q == '') {
			url = '//www.soku.com?inner' + ('&' + stat);
		} else {
			if (this.form.action.indexOf('/q_') === -1) {
				q = encodeURIComponent(q);
				url = this.form.action + '/q_' + q + ('?' + stat);
			} else {
				url = this.form.action + ('&' + stat);
			}
		}
		window.open(url);
		this.form.action = '//www.soku.com/search_video';
		return false;
	}
}

	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>

				url = this.form.action + '/q_' + q + ('?' + stat);
			} else {
				url = this.form.action + ('&' + stat);
			}
		}
		window.open(url);
		this.form.action = '//www.soku.com/search_video';
		return false;
	}
}
</script>

<div name="m_pos" id="m_215516">
	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>
</div>


</div>

                    domlist1[i].innerHTML = '';

<div name="m_pos" id="m_215516">
	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>
</div>

<div name="m_pos" id="m_215516">
	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>

<div name="m_pos" id="m_215516">
	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>

	doSearch: function () {
		this.form = document.getElementById('qheader_search');
		if(!this.form){ return; }
		this.input = this.form.getElementsByTagName('input')[0];
		var q = this.trim(this.input.value), url = '',
				stat = 'spm=a2hww.20023042.#qheader_search~10';
		if (window.logPvid) {
			stat += '&_rp=' + window.logPvid;
		}

		if (q == '') {
			url = '//www.soku.com?inner' + ('&' + stat);
		} else {
			if (this.form.action.indexOf('/q_') === -1) {
				q = encodeURIComponent(q);
				url = this.form.action + '/q_' + q + ('?' + stat);
			} else {
				url = this.form.action + ('&' + stat);
			}
		}
		window.open(url);
		this.form.action = '//www.soku.com/search_video';
		return false;
	}
}

                        window.ikuDownloadIng = false;

                    return false;
                })
	});
})(jQuery);
</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>

var ykQHeader = {
	ltrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /^(\s*|ã*)/, "") },
	rtrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /(\s*|ã*)$/, "") },
	trim:function(s){ return this.ltrim(this.rtrim(s));},
	doSearch: function () {
		this.form = document.getElementById('qheader_search');
		if(!this.form){ return; }
		this.input = this.form.getElementsByTagName('input')[0];
		var q = this.trim(this.input.value), url = '',
				stat = 'spm=a2hww.20023042.#qheader_search~10';
		if (window.logPvid) {
			stat += '&_rp=' + window.logPvid;
		}

		if (q == '') {
			url = '//www.soku.com?inner' + ('&' + stat);
		} else {
			if (this.form.action.indexOf('/q_') === -1) {
				q = encodeURIComponent(q);
				url = this.form.action + '/q_' + q + ('?' + stat);
			} else {
				url = this.form.action + ('&' + stat);
			}
		}
		window.open(url);
		this.form.action = '//www.soku.com/search_video';
		return false;
	}
}

	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>

                        window.location.href += '&screen=phone';
                }else{
                        window.location.href += '?screen=phone';
                }
        }
}

var ykQHeader = {
	ltrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /^(\s*|ã*)/, "") },
	rtrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /(\s*|ã*)$/, "") },
	trim:function(s){ return this.ltrim(this.rtrim(s));},
	doSearch: function () {
		this.form = document.getElementById('qheader_search');
		if(!this.form){ return; }
		this.input = this.form.getElementsByTagName('input')[0];
		var q = this.trim(this.input.value), url = '',
				stat = 'spm=a2hww.20023042.#qheader_search~10';
		if (window.logPvid) {
			stat += '&_rp=' + window.logPvid;
		}

		if (q == '') {
			url = '//www.soku.com?inner' + ('&' + stat);
		} else {
			if (this.form.action.indexOf('/q_') === -1) {
				q = encodeURIComponent(q);
				url = this.form.action + '/q_' + q + ('?' + stat);
			} else {
				url = this.form.action + ('&' + stat);
			}
		}
		window.open(url);
		this.form.action = '//www.soku.com/search_video';
		return false;
	}
}

	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>

	ltrim:function(s){ return s.replace( /^(\s*|ã*)/, "") },

	doSearch: function () {
		this.form = document.getElementById('qheader_search');
		if(!this.form){ return; }
		this.input = this.form.getElementsByTagName('input')[0];
		var q = this.trim(this.input.value), url = '',
				stat = 'spm=a2hww.20023042.#qheader_search~10';

               $("#ikuDownLoad").on('click', function (evt) {
                    if (window.ikuDownloadIng) return false;
                    var target =this;
                    if (!target) {
                        return false;

<div name="m_pos" id="m_215516">
	<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
$(document).ready(function(){

	var $ykthumbPage = $('.yk-slide');
	var $thumbPos = $('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $btnroll =$ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-pages');
	var $ykPrev = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnprev');
	var $ykNext = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-slide-btnnext');
	var $ykcol4 = $ykthumbPage.find('.yk-col4');

	var iWidth = 220 * $ykcol4.length; // æ»å®½åº¦
	var iW = $ykthumbPage.width()+20-110; // ä¸å±çå®½åº¦
	var totalPage = Math.ceil(iWidth/iW);
	var i = 0;

	$btnroll.css('width',iWidth);

	// å¦æä¸å¤ä¸å±ï¼åéèç¿»é¡µæé®
	if ( iWidth <= iW ) {
		$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
		$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
	}

	$ykPrev.click(function(){//å·¦è¾¹çæé®
		var cur_i = --i;
		if ( cur_i > 0 ) {
			var rightpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:rightpos});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
		} else {
			$thumbPos.animate({left:0});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykNext.css('visibility','visible');
			i = 0;
		}
	});

	$ykNext.click(function(){//å³è¾¹
		var cur_i = ++i;
		if(cur_i+1 < totalPage){
			var leftpos = -iW * cur_i;
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftpos});
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
		}else{
			var leftlast = -(iWidth - iW);
			$thumbPos.animate({left:leftlast});
			$ykNext.css('visibility','hidden');
			$ykPrev.css('visibility','visible');
			i = totalPage-1;
		}
	});

});
})(jQuery);
</script>
</div>

    var loadScript = function(src, callback) {
        var script = document.createElement('script'),
        head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        script.type = 'text/javascript';
        script.charset = 'UTF-8';
        script.src = src;
        if (script.addEventListener) {
            script.addEventListener('load',
            function() {
                callback();
            },
            false);
        } else if (script.attachEvent) {
            script.attachEvent('onreadystatechange',
            function() {
                var target = window.event.srcElement;
                if (target.readyState == 'loaded') {
                    callback();
                }
            });
        }
        head.appendChild(script);
    };

    var loadScript = function(src, callback) {
        var script = document.createElement('script'),
        head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        script.type = 'text/javascript';
        script.charset = 'UTF-8';
        script.src = src;
        if (script.addEventListener) {
            script.addEventListener('load',
            function() {
                callback();
            },
            false);
        } else if (script.attachEvent) {
            script.attachEvent('onreadystatechange',
            function() {
                var target = window.event.srcElement;
                if (target.readyState == 'loaded') {
                    callback();
                }
            });
        }
        head.appendChild(script);
    };

var language = document.__language__ || (navigator.language && navigator.language.indexOf("en") > -1 ? "en" : "");
    var loadScript = function(src, callback) {
        var script = document.createElement('script'),
        head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        script.type = 'text/javascript';
        script.charset = 'UTF-8';
        script.src = src;
        if (script.addEventListener) {
            script.addEventListener('load',
            function() {
                callback();
            },
            false);
        } else if (script.attachEvent) {
            script.attachEvent('onreadystatechange',
            function() {
                var target = window.event.srcElement;
                if (target.readyState == 'loaded') {
                    callback();
                }
            });
        }
        head.appendChild(script);
    };
    var scene = "";
    if (navigator.userAgent.match(/.*(iPhone|iPad|Android|ios|SymbianOS|Windows Phone).*/i)) {
        scene = "register_h5";

            language:language,
            callback: function(data) {
                document.getElementById("nc-session-id").value = data.csessionid;
                document.getElementById("nc-sig").value = data.sig;
                document.getElementById("nc-verify-form").submit();
            }
        });
    }

    var loadScript = function(src, callback) {
        var script = document.createElement('script'),
        head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        script.type = 'text/javascript';
        script.charset = 'UTF-8';
        script.src = src;
        if (script.addEventListener) {
            script.addEventListener('load',
            function() {
                callback();
            },
            false);
        } else if (script.attachEvent) {
            script.attachEvent('onreadystatechange',
            function() {
                var target = window.event.srcElement;
                if (target.readyState == 'loaded') {
                    callback();
                }
            });
        }
        head.appendChild(script);
    };

        loadScript('//g.alicdn.com/sd/ncpc/nc.js', ncinitpc);
    }
    function ncinitpc() {
        UA_Opt.Flag = 880846;
        document.getElementById("nocaptcha").style.cssText = "margin-top:-10px";
        noCaptcha({
            renderTo: "#nocaptcha",
            appkey: "X82Y__54aa8e5fba28e1386bf36db82e6d3b28",
            token: "0dfd3ded5f47b1763ff203d4e71fd840",
            scene: scene,
            is_Opt: 1,
            language:language,
            callback: function(data) {
                document.getElementById("nc-session-id").value = data.csessionid;
                document.getElementById("nc-sig").value = data.sig;
                document.getElementById("nc-verify-form").submit();
            }
        });
    }
    function ncinit() {
        UA_Opt.Flag = 880846;
        NoCaptcha.init({
            renderTo: "#nocaptcha",

                document.getElementById("nc-sig").value = data.sig;
                document.getElementById("nc-verify-form").submit();
            }
        });
        NoCaptcha.setEnabled(true);
    }
